  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_ce1e9d64-a31f-4328-917a-c3cbbaf5d75a'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

Vaughan (<i>The Private Eye</i>, <i>Y: The Last Man</i>) and Fiona Staples (<i>North 40</i>, <i>Red Sonja</i>), Saga is the sweeping tale of one young family fighting to find their place in the universe. Searching for their literary hero, new parents Marko and Alana travel to a cosmic lighthouse on the planet Quietus, while the couple's multiple pursuers fi</span>
  <span id="freeText6593675239640491698" style="display:none">From the <u>Hugo Award</u>-winning duo of Brian K. Vaughan (<i>The Private Eye</i>, <i>Y: The Last Man</i>) and Fiona Staples (<i>North 40</i>, <i>Red Sonja</i>), Saga is the sweeping tale of one young family fighting to find their place in the universe. Searching for their literary hero, new parents Marko and Alana travel to a cosmic lighthouse on the planet Quietus, while the couple's multiple pursuers finally close in on their targets.<br /><br /><b>Collecting</b>: <i>Saga</i> 13-18.</span>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2368517034514411881">This comic is so good it's starting to piss me off. <br/><br/>Dear Mr. Vaughan, <br/><br/>You should not be able to make me cry five times in the same fucking comic. I just love that there is a book and author in these graphic novels. CLASSIC! <br/><br/>Grandma Klara decides she's going too! They will not leave her behind. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458434226i/18488621._SX540_.jpg' alt=' : ' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Of course things don't go so well when they first get there as Klara gets one of her ears ate off by some bugs. Joyful! But after they find their author, he's drunk at first, they all get a long and I</span>
  <span id="freeText1990182581891019490" style="display:none">MY BLOG: <a href="http://melissa413readsalot.blogspot.com/2016/03/saga-volume-3-by-brian-k-vaughan-fiona.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Melissa Martin's Reading List</a><br><br>In this volume Alana and Marko decide they are going to go looking for the author of the romance book they read. I just love that there is a book and author in these graphic novels. CLASSIC! <br><br>Grandma Klara decides she's going too! They will not leave her behind. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458434226i/18488621._SX540_.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Of course things don't go so well when they first get there as Klara gets one of her ears ate off by some bugs. Joyful! But after they find their author, he's drunk at first, they all get a long and I was hoping good things could start happening for everyone. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458434226i/18488622._SX540_.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>That never happens does it....<br><br>Meanwhile, The Will, Gwen, the little girl and lying cat are trapped on a planet that if you eat the fruit you will have hallucinations that make you want to stay there. Oh and this guy/tv head. ↓<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458434226i/18488624._SX540_.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He gets his clock ticked for a bit. <br><br>You have a show down with Marko, Gwen and Alana. Crap goes all to hell and everyone runs off on different missions. I can't say any more. <br><br>I can't wait to see what all kinds of cray cray is going to go on in the next one. I'm trying to read them slowly as I have the newest one on pre-order :-D Yay! <br><br>The little picture at the end where it shows Hazel walking is precious! <br><br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11706735489074426707">These books are like Prozac..I just want to eat them up by the dozen.<br/>I think this one is even better than Volume 2. (Yes, I still haven't gotten vol. 1 yet)<br/><br/>Our heroes Marco and Alana have gone to find their literary hero so that they can ask him questions about the book that caused them to become a couple.<br/><a href='http://imgur.com/t7gBwFW' rel='nofollow noopener'>

  <span id="freeText11706735489074426707" style="display:none">These books are like Prozac..I just want to eat them up by the dozen.<br>I think this one is even better than Volume 2. (Yes, I still haven't gotten vol. 1 yet)<br><br>Our heroes Marco and Alana have gone to find their literary hero so that they can ask him questions about the book that caused them to become a couple.<br><a href="http://imgur.com/t7gBwFW" rel="nofollow noopener">

              <span id="reviewTextContainer2419531909" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6357985846108435029">The weirdness continues in the third volume of this excellent series. <br/><br/>I must admit, I expected it to lose its dazzling nature after the first volume but none of its awesomeness has diminished. I have high hopes that it will remain persistently good unlike so many other comics that fluctuate in quality.<br/><br/>The best thing about this volume is a cyclops author who knows how to make a fucking great entrance and a lasting impression: <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1528652078i/25711767._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1528652078i/25711768._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>And from here the first few issues fall into discussions about the impo</span>
  <span id="freeText6357985846108435029" style="display:none">The weirdness continues in the third volume of this excellent series. <br><br>I must admit, I expected it to lose its dazzling nature after the first volume but none of its awesomeness has diminished. I have high hopes that it will remain persistently good unlike so many other comics that fluctuate in quality.<br><br>The best thing about this volume is a cyclops author who knows how to make a fucking great entrance and a lasting impression: <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1528652078i/25711767._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1528652078i/25711768._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And from here the first few issues fall into discussions about the importance of literature (even in a war torn world full of aliens, monsters and sexual deviants like this one.)Books can change the world and one particular book by this crazy cyclops man has brought the two central characters together, which led them to his door to seek answers about what do next. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474374869i/20590438._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And of course even weirder shit follows them and it all ends rather quickly. As well written as the majority of the characters are in here, it’s great to see them get killed off in random ways. It bodes very well at this stage that the author is willing to kill when he needs to.<br><br>I really hope this series never loses its momentum. Bring on volume four!</span>

        <a title="Kemper" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kemper" href="/user/show/405390-kemper">Kemper</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer933099100" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4695490368526589155">Just your typical story about a couple from opposing species of an interstellar war falling in love and having a baby, then fleeing the governments and hired mercenaries of both sides in a wooden rocketship with their ghost babysitter...<br/><br/>Three volumes in and so far each one has been 5 stars. I'm pretty sure that has never happened to me before. <br/></span>

<div id="review_1712229569" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1712229569" />
    <a title="Melanie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3030788-melanie"><img alt="Melanie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577914102p2/3030788.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1712229569?book_show_action=true">Jul 28, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melanie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melanie" href="/user/show/3030788-melanie">Melanie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=graphic-novels">graphic-novels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=dark">dark</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=magic">magic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=read-in-2016">read-in-2016</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1712229569" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2839608242045749039"><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1644076193?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>Vol. 1</a> ★★★★<br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1644287873' rel='nofollow noopener'>Vol. 2</a> ★★★★<br/><br/>This graphic novel made me more emotional than any other graphic novel ever has. This third installment will really pull on your heartstrings, so be prepared to feel all the feels. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458434226i/18488621._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This graphic novel also deals with some pretty BIG themes: <br/>- Being able to love after a loss. <br/>- Following your dreams, no matter what.<br/>- How important, and memorable, it is to read to young children. <br/>- Society's views on the LGBT community, and how much it needs to change. <br/>- And most importantly, </span>
  <span id="freeText2839608242045749039" style="display:none"><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1644076193?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Vol. 1</a> ★★★★<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1644287873" rel="nofollow noopener">Vol. 2</a> ★★★★<br><br>This graphic novel made me more emotional than any other graphic novel ever has. This third installment will really pull on your heartstrings, so be prepared to feel all the feels. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458434226i/18488621._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This graphic novel also deals with some pretty BIG themes: <br>- Being able to love after a loss. <br>- Following your dreams, no matter what.<br>- How important, and memorable, it is to read to young children. <br>- Society's views on the LGBT community, and how much it needs to change. <br>- And most importantly, <b>your worth is not dependent on the abuse you have suffered.</b> You can heal and relearn your worth after sexual, physical, and/or mental abuse. <br><br>This volume was fantastic and, hands down, my favorite so far! I love Marko and Alana so very much, yet, I love Hazel even more. Her voice is perfect, and I love seeing the journey/struggle of her childhood. Sophie is the other shining-light of this series, to me. I can't wait to follow both of these two young girls' journeys for three more volumes. <i>Saga</i> is very quickly becoming the best graphic novel series I've ever read. <br><br>I'm now going to break down each chapter in this bind up. There will be <b>SPOILERS</b>, so please use caution in continuing if you have <i>not</i> read this graphic-novel, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1644076193?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Vol. 1</a>, or <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1644287873" rel="nofollow noopener">Vol. 2</a>!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418762318i/12889631._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>	<br><b>
  <u>CHAPTER THIRTEEN:</u>
</b><br>Kiara, Marko's mom, is still with our main characters on their tree-ship! She's still mourning the death of her husband at the end of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1644287873" rel="nofollow noopener">Vol. 2</a>. The ship is on their way to visit Marko and Alana's favorite author, D. Oswald Heist, who lives in a lighthouse. <br><br>The Will, Gwendolyn, Sophie, and Lying Cat are still searching for Marko and Alana, but the Will is starting to have his doubts, because he is seeing the Stalk. <br><br><b>
  <u>CHAPTER FOURTEEN:</u>
</b><br>We are introduced to two reporters, Lipsher and Doff, who are trying to break the case on Alana's motives. They are poking their noses in anything that resembles a lead on a story, and even visit her step-mom, Even. <br><br>The tree-ship lands and everyone meets D. Oswald Heist, who ends up being a pretty great guy. <br><br><b>
  <u>CHAPTER FIFTEEN:</u>
</b><br>Countess Robot X, Alana's first commanding officer, is interviewed by Lipsher and Doff, and they start to realize this story about Alana might be much bigger than they originally even thought. <br><br>Sophie stabs the Will, and it doesn't look like he has long to live. The food on the island they were on was making them all hallucinate, and Sophie's hallucination made her stab the Will. <br><br>Marko and crew have officially bonded with Mr. Heist , and seeing their family fun warmed my heart to no end. <br><br><b>
  <u>CHAPTER SIXTEEN:</u>
</b><br>The story these reporters are piecing together is getting scary, and someone calls to have them get "taken care of". The Will is the first choice, but since he is no longer accepting clients the job gets assigned to the Brand. <br><br>Alana expresses her love for acting and theater and Marko is very supportive. Then, the Prince Robot IV confrontation we see with Mr. Heist in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1644287873" rel="nofollow noopener">Vol. 2</a> comes into play. <br><br>The Will is still dying, so Gwen decides that Marko is her only chance at saving him, so she rushes to the lighthouse. <br><br><b>
  <u>CHAPTER SEVENTEEN:</u>
</b><br>The Brand meets with the reporters, while Prince Robot IV deals with his sexuality.<br><br>Mr. Heist dies by the hands of Gwen, and completely broke my heart for Kiara. <br><br><b>
  <u>CHAPTER EIGHTEEN:</u>
</b><br>Prince Robot IV is a little fried. Gwen confronts Marko and Alana like the crazy bitch that she is, but thankfully Alana and Marko's trust runs much deeper than Gwen expects. <br><br>We find out the Brand is the Will's sister, and that he named Sophie after her, and I could barely see the last panels because of all my tears. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1471223599i/20013082._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm so excited for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1728454805?type=review#rating_85607252" rel="nofollow noopener">Vol. 4</a>, because we find out that Marko, Alana, and Hazel have had a few months of calmer happiness, therefore, in the next installment Hazel will be much bigger, and walking! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423234809i/13599373._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="https://meltotheany.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.twitter.com/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://meltotheany.tumblr.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Tumblr</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/meltotheany/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UC4RbHEg_fH6CewJrh_0xJ9g" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a> | <a href="http://www.twitch.tv/meltotheany/profile" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitch</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="2839608242045749039" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3454741679" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15073465641020523018">The art style in <i>Saga</i> never fails to impress me. This was a really entertaining volume!<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>“After years of pitched battles, my father was ready for a significantly less stressful career. Unfortunately, he decided to try raising a girl.”</i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>Marko and Alana are always fun protagonists to follow, especially when paired with intergalactic warfare and mutant creatures around every corner. In this instalment the pair are on a mission to find their idol, who may also be able to assist them greatly.<br/><br/>While th</span>
  <span id="freeText15073465641020523018" style="display:none">The art style in <i>Saga</i> never fails to impress me. This was a really entertaining volume!<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“After years of pitched battles, my father was ready for a significantly less stressful career. Unfortunately, he decided to try raising a girl.”</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />Marko and Alana are always fun protagonists to follow, especially when paired with intergalactic warfare and mutant creatures around every corner. In this instalment the pair are on a mission to find their idol, who may also be able to assist them greatly.<br /><br />While the plot didn’t progress as much as I would have liked this volume, the characters did undergo a good amount of development. There were several twists that left me completely shocked, which made for a quick reading experience. An overall great addition to the series!</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2113592675" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer13009435912756581616">I think this was my least-favorite so far. While it had its moments, it felt like not a whole lot happened until the end. <br/><br/>I think Gwendolyn looks awesome and is bad-ass, but she is also kind of one-dimensional and the jilted lover act is not my favorite. Plus, she doesn't seem very mature, she reacts without thinking. It's just annoying.<br/><br/>It felt like not a lot happened on Quietus besides philosophical conversations about war and family. <br/><br/>I really like The Will and Lying Cat.<br/><br/>The Brand intrigues me.</span>
  <span id="freeText13009435912756581616" style="display:none">I think this was my least-favorite so far. While it had its moments, it felt like not a whole lot happened until the end. <br><br>I think Gwendolyn looks awesome and is bad-ass, but she is also kind of one-dimensional and the jilted lover act is not my favorite. Plus, she doesn't seem very mature, she reacts without thinking. It's just annoying.<br><br>It felt like not a lot happened on Quietus besides philosophical conversations about war and family. <br><br>I really like The Will and Lying Cat.<br><br>The Brand intrigues me.<br><br>I don't really care for the side plot with the two investigative reporters.<br><br>I'm wondering if the reveal that <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Alana is an undercover spy is true.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>I think my very favorite scene was when Sophie (Slave Girl) was with Lying Cat talking and says something about her being dirty because of all the things she had done to her and had to do and Lying Cat interrupts her ---<i> "Lying."</i> And Sophie smiles and cuddles Lying Cat. Awwwww.<br><br>The art on the back with Marko and Alana posing like a bodice ripper cover was great!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506264111i/24001739._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I hope we get more evolution and growth of the main characters. Hazel is adorable, obviously, but there really weren't too many parts with her either, except as decorating a scene here and there. *shrug*</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_851800554" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/851800554" />
    <a title="Algernon (Darth Anyan)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4728718-algernon-darth-anyan"><img alt="Algernon (Darth Anyan)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1553101944p2/4728718.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/851800554?book_show_action=true">Feb 11, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Algernon (Darth Anyan)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Algernon (Darth Anyan)" href="/user/show/4728718-algernon-darth-anyan">Algernon (Darth Anyan)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4728718-algernon-darth-anyan?shelf=comics">comics</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4728718-algernon-darth-anyan?shelf=2014">2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer851800554" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11238191922883648473"><br/>Three stars might seem a bit harsh for one of the best adult comics published today, but it reflects my disappointment with how little actual content there was in this third story arc. There simply isn't enough meat on the bare bones of the adventure to justify calling it space opera or even epic. It feels more like a resume, a synopsis of the actual events. I finished it all in a couple of hours on a Sunday afternoon, and now I have to wait until the end of the year for the next story arc to be</span>
  <span id="freeText11238191922883648473" style="display:none"><br />Three stars might seem a bit harsh for one of the best adult comics published today, but it reflects my disappointment with how little actual content there was in this third story arc. There simply isn't enough meat on the bare bones of the adventure to justify calling it space opera or even epic. It feels more like a resume, a synopsis of the actual events. I finished it all in a couple of hours on a Sunday afternoon, and now I have to wait until the end of the year for the next story arc to be completed (I refuse to read monthly installments for the same reason: too little material - just whetting my appetite for more and then leaving me hanging). At this rate the series will take longer than A Song of Ice and Fire to reach the finish line.<br /><br />I think it is fair to say I would not be so disappointed if I didn't actually like what I read. I believe the awards and the praise <b>Saga</b> is receiving are entirely deserved, especially for the artwork of Fiona Staple. The worldbuilding, what little we have seen of it so far, is also excellent. Vaughn manages to insert strong social commentary and anti-war messages in the conversations between characters.<br /><br />As for the third story arc itself: Romeo and Juliet, a.k.a. Marko and Alana, two deserters from opposing armies in the galactic war, are hiding with their newborn daughter in the house of a one-eyed writer (Futurama reference for geeks?). They are pursued by a robot-head Prince, by a bountyhunter with a telepathic cat, by a vengeful ex-girlfriend and, newly introduced here, a couple of scandal journalists. The build up is slow, but the resolution is well handled, closing this particular arc at a good point and promising interesting developments in the future.<br /><br />I saved one quote that I particularly enjoyed, as the writer is reading extremely horrible fairytales to the little girl:<br /><br /><i> All good children's stories are the same: young creature breaks rules, has incredible adventure, then returns home with the knowledge that aforementioned rules are there for a reson.<br />Of course, the <b>actual</b> message to the careful reader is: break the rules as often as you can because who the hell doesn't want to have an adventure.</i><br /><br />Recommended for very patient readers, willing to invest the time waiting for the next issues.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11238191922883648473" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1844410464" />
    <a title="Petrik" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/59458347-petrik"><img alt="Petrik" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1568016775p2/59458347.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1844410464?book_show_action=true">Dec 21, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Petrik" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Petrik" href="/user/show/59458347-petrik">Petrik</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1844410464" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10065795705593603668">Buddy reading this entire series with my favorite <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/celeste57' rel='nofollow noopener'>Princess Celeste</a><br/><br/>I'm blazing through this series and even though I'm enjoying it, I still don't get why the series is so highly acclaimed. It could be just me but I really wish this books doesn't have any actions at all, the story gets better, characters are explored more but every time there's an action going on the art really made me feel detached. Even though I prefer there's no action, in this book there's a quote "it will be action packed." t</span>
  <span id="freeText10065795705593603668" style="display:none">Buddy reading this entire series with my favorite <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/celeste57" rel="nofollow noopener">Princess Celeste</a><br /><br />I'm blazing through this series and even though I'm enjoying it, I still don't get why the series is so highly acclaimed. It could be just me but I really wish this books doesn't have any actions at all, the story gets better, characters are explored more but every time there's an action going on the art really made me feel detached. Even though I prefer there's no action, in this book there's a quote "it will be action packed." turns out there's only 2 exchange of shots -_-' that's not action packed at all! <br /><br />I'm not blaming the art in general, only during the actions, it always made me laugh cause it looked kinda awkward. Other than that everything is gorgeous, the world, the characters were well drawn and I love the ending to volume 3. The series is good don't get me wrong, I just wish it's better than this seeing the raving reviews on it. I hope the next book will change my opinion.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10065795705593603668" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText1829227618572292155" style="display:none">Re-Read 5/13/18:<br /><br />I cried a little. I just got all choked up. Again.<br /><br />I cannot understand just how attached to these guys I've gotten. All of them. Every single last character. It's like I'm under a spell. A deep, dark spell.<br /><br />And then, to top it all off, EVERY SINGLE PERSON REFERENCED becomes ALIVE and BEAUTIFUL later! I swear, this is only getting better every time I read it. :) The whole thing. Is. Blowing Me Away. :)<br /><br /><br />Original Review:<br /><br />I agree with the goddamned writer on this one. Don't kill your darlings. Kill off everyone else until all who are left are your most precious ones.<br /><br />Still, I'm going to miss the one whom the narrative left behind. I loved that old bastard.<br /><br />I loved the surprises. I was pretty shocked at the directions they took and can't fault the logic...</span>

<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('qmqVegsx8x+9n5BuqIF4XO1y/WUJRY1ldM4LZ8J0i38TepLYEuGKT418h5K74N14Wankav/ujNRY2mQ2Cig7Lw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Sui/RWGayMP+tKdOxxIra9ZZ1Q5GyD54VXxUzrc6rJPz+LjneEqxk85XsLLUc45PYoLMAbBjP8l5aDuff2Ycww==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

  <span id="freeText8233530187689001618" style="display:none">Brian K. Vaughan is the writer and co-creator of comic-book series including SAGA, PAPER GIRLS, Y THE LAST MAN, RUNAWAYS, and most recently, BARRIER, a digital comic with artist Marcos Martin about immigration, available from their pay-what-you-want site <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.PanelSyndicate.com">www.PanelSyndicate.com</a><br /><br />BKV's work has been recognized at the Eisner, Harvey, Hugo, Shuster, Eagle, and British Fantasy Awards. He sometimes writes for film and television in Los Angeles, where he lives with his family and their dogs Hamburger and Milkshake. </span>
